 , Hosilkar told 'india Today' that it is very important to name the cyclone

 India falls in the southern region of the world
 kul aath desh is samooh main aate hai or ve ek-ek karke baari baari se chakravaati tufaanon kaa naam dete hai

 If you want to give a name to a cyclonic storm, then its method is simple
 mausam vibhaag ne bataaya ki agar log naam dena chaahate hai to use list main shaamil kar liya jaataa he

 It is also taken care that its name should not be sensitive nor inflammatory

 Ayodhya Case: a five-judge bench has given a historic verdict on Saturday on the Ayodhya land dispute
 supreme court ne kaha ki sunni vakf board vivaadit dhaanche par apana exclusive rhite sabit nahin kar paaya
 The court has ruled to give the disputed structure land to the Hindu side
 saath hi sarkaar se kaha he ki vah musalamaanon ko ayodhya main hi duusari jagah paanch acre jameen de
 This decision of the Supreme Court can prove to be a big step to reduce the deadlock between the two communities over the past several decades
 saath hi paanch jajon kii sanvaidhanik peeth ne kaha ki yah nyaayalay ek aise vivaad ke samaadhaan ke liye kaam kar rahaa he jisaki utpatti bharat ke vichaar ke samaan puraani he
 While giving the verdict at the disputed site, the bench has also pointed out the points on which it has given the verdict
 aaie ek najar daalate hue un binduon par jo supreme court ke is faisla kaa aadhaar bane-court ne faisla sunaate hue kaha kisubaton ke aadhaar
 The Muslim side has not been able to prove its exclusive right on the disputed structure better than the Hindus
 “22 / 23 disambar 1949 ko muslimon ko masjid se bedakhal kar diya tha, jise aakhir main 6 disambar 1992 ko dhaha diya gaya
 Despite this the Muslims did not leave the mosque
 nyaayalay musalamaanon kii andekha nahin karegaa, jinhen vanchiton kii tarah rakhaa gaya he
 This is not true in a secular nation committed to the rule of law
 isbare main supreme ne kaha ki vivaadit bhoomi kaa vibhaajan kanoonee rup se asthir tha
 Also, it is not possible to maintain social peace
 elahabaad hoicourt kii tarah iskaa samaadhaan sambhav nahin he
 The division of land will not protect the interests of both the parties and will not preserve a lasting sense of peace
